<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">fremdgehen</i>. ***vrek.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:vrek.html>vrek</a> (19280)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">vrec</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:vrek.html>vrek</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*frek</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-West_Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-West Germanic language">Proto-West Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*frek</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*frekaz</i>. Cognate to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">frech</i> (Old High German <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">freh</i>), <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">frec</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vrek.html>vrek</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vrekken.html>vrekken</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vrek.html>vrekje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">scrooge</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">miser</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:boer.html>Boer</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:munten.html>Munte</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vreselijk.html>vreselijke</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:vrek.html>vrek</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zoon.html>zoon</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:snoep.html>snoep</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:noch.html>noch</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:speelgoed.html>speelgoed</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gunt.html>gunt</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Farmer Coyn <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a terrible <b>miser</b>, who <a href = vnd.unilang:lets.html>lets</a> his son have candy nor toys.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">vrient</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">friund</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*frijōndz</i>. Related to the verb <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vrijen.html>vrijen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to make love; to be in a relationship</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:vriendelijk.html>vriendelijk</a> (1714)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">vrintlec</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">vriendelijc</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*friuntlik</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*friuntlik</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*frijōndlīkaz</i>, equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vriend.html>vriend</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-lijk</i>. Cognate to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">freundlich</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">friendly</i>.

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">vriesen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*friesan</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-West_Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-West Germanic language">Proto-West Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*freusan</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*freusaną</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*prews-</i>.
</p>

***vrij.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:vrij.html>vrij</a> (425)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">vri</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">frī</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*frijaz</i>, which derives from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*PreyH-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to be fond of</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Related to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vrijen.html>vrijen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to love</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vrijdag.html>vrijdag</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">friday</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vriend.html>vriend</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">friend</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vrouw.html>vrouw</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">woman</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, and <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vrede.html>vrede</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">peace</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vrij.html>vrij</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vrijer.html>vrijer</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">vrijst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>free; not imprisoned or enslaved.

<li>free; unconstrained.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>hij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vrije.html>vrije</a> hand <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:land.html>land</a></i> ― <span class="e-translation">he <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> a free hand <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a> the <a href = vnd.unilang:land.html>land</a></span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>free; unobstructed, without blockages.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:afvoer.html>afvoer</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vrij.html>vrij</a></i> ― <span class="e-translation">the drain <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> unobstructed</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>free; without obligations.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:vrijdag.html>vrijdag</a> (1698)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">vrīdach</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">vriendach</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*frīadag</i>, from late <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*Frijjōz dagaz</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">day of Frigg</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, calque of Latin <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:dies.html>dies</a> Veneris</i>.
</p><p>Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German">Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds">Freedag</i>, German <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">Freitag</i>, West Frisian <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy"><a href = vnd.unilang:freed.html>freed</a></i>, English <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">Friday</i>, Danish <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">fredag</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vrijdag.html>vrijdag</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vrijdag.html>vrijdagen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vrijdag.html>vrijdagje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>Friday</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:vrijdag.html>vrijdag</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span>
</p>
<ol><li><span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(tijdrekening)</span>, <span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(<a href = vnd.unilang:dag.html>dag</a>)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:dag.html>dag</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> week <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:na.html>na</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:donderdag.html>donderdag</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zaterdag.html>zaterdag</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:komt.html>komt</a>
<dl><dd><ul><li><i><b><a href = vnd.unilang:vrijdag.html>Vrijdag</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ben.html>ben</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:volgens.html>volgens</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:mij.html>mij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vrij.html>vrij</a>.</i> </li></ul></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vrij.html>vrij</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:denken.html>denken</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dictatoriaal.html>-er</a></i>, calque of  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">freethinker</i>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:vrijen.html>vrijen</a> (2530)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">vrien</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*frīon</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*frijōną</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to love</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vrijen.html>vrijen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to make love, to have sex <span class="defdate">[from 20th century]</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:heel.html>heel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:belangrijk.html>belangrijk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:om.html>om</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:veilig.html>veilig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:vrijen.html>vrijen</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">It's very important to <b>have</b> safe <b>sex</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl>
<ul><li><b>2008</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/nl:Bram_Bakker" class="extiw" title="w:nl:Bram Bakker">Bram <a href = vnd.unilang:bakker.html>Bakker</a></a>, “Weg <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dr.html>Dr</a>. Atkins”, in: <i><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dwarse.html>dwarse</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:psychiater.html>psychiater</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:uitgeverij.html>Uitgeverij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:maart.html>Maarten</a> Muntinga, Amsterdam, →ISBN
<dl><dd><a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>En</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:partners.html>partners</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:krijgen.html>krijgen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:echte.html>echte</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:reden.html>reden</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:horen.html>horen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:waarom.html>waarom</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:er.html>er</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zo.html>zo</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:weinig.html>weinig</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:vrijen.html>gevreeën</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:wordt.html>wordt</a>.
<dl><dd>And <a href = vnd.unilang:partners.html>partners</a> don’<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> get to hear the real reason why not much <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> happening in <a href = vnd.unilang:bed.html>bed</a>.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to make out, to cuddle, to hug and kiss
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zij.html>Zij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vroeg.html>vroeg</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:haar.html>haar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vriendje.html>vriendje</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:om.html>om</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:eerst.html>eerst</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gewoon.html>gewoon</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:vrijen.html>vrijen</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">She asked her boyfriend to just <b>kiss and hug</b> first.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to have a relationship, to be a couple, to go out with someone
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zij.html>Zij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:heeft.html>heeft</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:haar.html>haar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vriend.html>vriend</a> Alex <a href = vnd.unilang:leren.html>leren</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kennen.html>kennen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> internet <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ze.html>ze</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:vrijen.html>vrijen</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:al.html>al</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:meer.html>meer</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dan.html>dan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:jaar.html>jaar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nu.html>nu</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">She <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> her boyfriend Alex on the Internet and now they've <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> <b>going out together</b> for more than a year already.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>The ambiguity between the first two senses often leads to confusion, which can lead the hearer to ask for clarification which sense <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> meant, but it also conveys exactly that the distinction might not be clear.
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:vrijend.html>vrijend</a> (62344)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***vrijgeleide.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:vrijgeleide.html>vrijgeleide</a> (27336)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vrij.html>vrij</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:geleide.html>geleide</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vrijgeleide.html>vrijgeleide</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vrijgeleide.html>vrijgeleiden</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl">vrijgeleides</b>)

***vrijkorps.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:vrijkorps.html>vrijkorps</a> (78252)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>First attested around 1783. From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vrij.html>vrij</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:korps.html>korps</a></i>, probably a calque of  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Freikorps</i>, attested a few years earlier.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vrijkorps.html>vrijkorps</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vrijkorps.html>vrijkorpsen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vrijkorps.html>vrijkorpsje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">paramilitary</span> group
<ul><li><b>1783</b> July 31, "<a href = vnd.unilang:zang.html>Zang</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:aan.html>aan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> Leydsche <a href = vnd.unilang:vrij.html>Vrij</a> Corps", in <i><a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>Op</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> loffelijke <a href = vnd.unilang:memorie.html>memorie</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:der.html>der</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:stad.html>stad</a> Leyden</i>.
<dl><dd><a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>Dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:uw.html>uw</a> <b>Vrijcorps</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:steeds.html>steeds</a> blijv' in ſtand, / <a href = vnd.unilang:tot.html>Tot</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nut.html>nut</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:stad.html>Stad</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vaderland.html>Vaderland</a>.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1786</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Elizabeth_Wolff-Dekker" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Elizabeth Wolff-Dekker">Elizabeth Bekker, <a href = vnd.unilang:wed.html>wed</a>. Wolff</a> <i><a href = vnd.unilang:vrijheid.html>Vrijheid</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:blijheid.html>blijheid</a>: Vaderlansch dichtstuk</i>, publ. by Isaac <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> Cleef, page 19.
<dl><dd><a href = vnd.unilang:nu.html>Nu</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:elk.html>elk</a> <i><b>Vrij-corps</b></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vrijheid.html>Vrijheid</a>, / <a href = vnd.unilang:alles.html>alles</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:---.html>---</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ook.html>ook</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:leven.html>leven</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:waagt.html>waagt</a>:</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">militia</span></li></ol>

***vrijwillig.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:vrijwillig.html>vrijwillig</a> (4918)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>16th century, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vrij.html>vrij</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">free</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wil.html>wil</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">will</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-ig</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">-y</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, probably after somewhat earlier <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">freiwillig</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vrijwillig.html>vrijwillig</a></strong> (<i>not comparable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>voluntary, of one's own free will</li></ol>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:vrijwillig.html>vrijwillig</a></b>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:vroom.html>vroom</a> (20643)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">vrōme</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">firm, upright</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, an adjective derived from the noun <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">vrōme</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">benefit, use</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*fruma</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*frumô</i>.

<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vrouw.html>vrouw</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mens.html>mens</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vrouwmens.html>vrouwmens</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> or <abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vrouwmens.html>vrouwmensen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vrouwmens.html>vrouwmensje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">now chiefly <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Belgium" class="extiw" title="w:Belgium">Belgium</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> neutral</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> woman</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Netherlands" class="extiw" title="w:Netherlands">Netherlands</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> derogatory</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> woman, bint</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>Use of the feminine gender <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> now archaic. The derogatory meaning, the most common meaning in the Netherlands, virtually always uses the neuter gender. Also compare the neuter usage at <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mens.html>mens</a></i>.

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:vrucht.html>vrucht</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">fruht</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">frūctus</i>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:vruchten.html>vruchte</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">forhta</i>. Ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*furhtį̄</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">fear</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*perg-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to frighten; fear</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vrucht.html>vrucht</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vruchten.html>vruchten</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vruchtje.html>vruchtje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
